name:L‚Äça‚Äçd‚Äçy‚Äç ‚Äçb‚Äçu‚Äçg‚Äçu‚Äça
info:Classic Garden Residence
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:9 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 19, 2024
msg:A very satisfying stay! This is my favorite hotel in Shanghai after visiting it countless times. This time, I accompanied my parents to visit friends and experienced the "Xing'anli Garden Hotel" in "Cheng Huan Ji". The lady at the front desk, Yan Tongxie, is beautiful, kind and professional. When she heard that we came here because of "Cheng Huan Ji", she directly upgraded us to the executive room of the VIP building, and also arranged the celebrity mansion guest room that is generally not booked to the public. Because "Cheng Huan Ji" was filmed in the Celebrity Mansion in Building 1. It's so loving! 
The Celebrity Mansion, built in 1917, was once the official residence of British businessman Mr. Malis. In 1927, Chiang Kai-shek and Soong Mei-ling held their engagement ceremony here and stayed. Comrade Chen Yi, the first mayor of Shanghai, also worked here during his term. In addition, there is a "Presidential Building" completed in 1920 in the hotel, where many foreign dignitaries including former US President Nixon and Prince William of the United Kingdom have stayed.
The hotel is in a very good location, close to Xintiandi, Sinan Mansions and the famous historical and cultural street of Wukang Road. We originally planned to walk around the city, but the hotel environment was too romantic and elegant, so we spent the whole day taking photos and walking around. My parents also praised the hotel. It was a perfect family trip! Thank you to all the hotel staff for providing us with such quality service.

       After this trip, I can only say that Ruijin Hotel deserves to be the State Guesthouse in Shanghai. The history of Ruijin Hotel seems to be unfolding in front of my eyes along with the breeze of the bungalow garden lawn: in 1927, it was the place where Soong Meiling got engaged, and in 1956, it officially became the reception venue of the Shanghai Municipal Party Committee. One of the places where he has received heads of state. In 1979, it was changed to Ruijin Hotel (one of the four major state hotels in Shanghai at the time).
        I am very grateful to every staff member of Ruijin Hotel. They are full of smiles and the service also shows the style of old Shanghai. The Shanghai dialect used when chatting with them and the retro lobby are even more Shanghai-style.
        Although the facilities are old, they are not old either. The old money style is vividly reflected in Ruijin Hotel. You may not be able to see it in the photos, but if you experience it once, you will know that Ruijin Hotel has put a lot of effort into maintaining it. They show that era. The sense of sophistication and high-end is difficult to experience in today's fast-paced era. Ruijin Hotel (InterContinental Hotel) deserves its name as a flagship store. The richness of history cannot be displayed by the so-called national style and simple hotels nowadays.
        If you have the chance, you will definitely come back to experience Ruijin Hotel. Strolling and drinking tea in Ruijin Hotel is really a rare and beautiful moment in life.

InterContinental Group entered Shanghai relatively early. The first InterContinental in China was the original New Asia Tomson InterContinental (later taken over by Jin Jiang). From the follow-up World Expo InterContinental, The National Convention and Exhibition Center InterContinental is the background of state-owned assets. Therefore, the management of Ruijin also agrees with each other. Among the high-end garden houses managed by state-owned assets in Shanghai in the early days, there were mainly four major groups "sharing", namely Donghu (suburbs: the western suburbs - construction businessman Yao Xizhou, Yao Naichi's villa - rebuilt 414 guest house after liberation, Chairman Mao went to Shanghai, Lived in Ruijin Hotel, Jinjiang Cultural Club and Xingguo Hotel. After the construction of 414 Guest House in 1960, Chairman Mao went to Shanghai 14 times from 1960 to 1967, and stayed in 414 Guest House every time. Dongjiao - Xinjian, Xingguo Radisson - The former site of the British merchant Taikoo foreign firm, now the old Dong‚Äôs house of the series of houses - The Opposite House - The Upper House - The Temple House - The Middle House, East Lake - Du Yuesheng, Lilac Garden - Li Hongzhang and Lilac, Hongqiao Guest House, are basically celebrities in the Republic of China period Former Residence Expansion), Jinjiang (Jinjiang Hotel, Cypress Hotel - Sassoon, Jing'an Hotel - Haiger Apar**ent) Hengshan (Hengshan - Picardy Apar**ent, Mahler Villa - Jewish Mahler,) New Asia Group has withdrawn from the hotel industry. The property was handed over to Jin Jiang for management.
Class 2 hotels are characterized by well-preserved historical buildings, exquisite gardens and large lawns, exotic designs, and legendary stories. In fact, there were many luxurious buildings in Shanghai during the Republic of China, but those with large gardens were rare. At present, these hotels are basically managed by state-owned assets. The Japanese garden Okura also belongs to this category. The original site of the French club was expanded, with a large lawn in front.
